usually happens in Figma when your objects are **inside a Frame or Auto Layout container** that’s constraining their position. A few ways to fix it:\\n\\n1. **Check if the frame has Auto Layout applied** \\n - Select the parent frame in the left layers panel. \\n - If you see *Auto Layout* properties in the right sidebar, that means elements are being auto-arranged. \\n - You can either: \\n - Remove Auto Layout (`Right-click → Remove Auto Layout`), or \\n - Adjust padding, spacing, and alignment to allow freer movement.\\n\\n2. **Detach the object from constraints** \\n - Select the object you want to move. \\n - Look at the right sidebar under **Constraints**. If it’s set to things like `Top \u0026 Left` or `Left \u0026 Right`, change it to **“Scale”** or just adjust to allow freer positioning.\\n\\n3. **Take it out of the frame** \\n - In the layers panel, drag your object **out of the frame** (drop it above or below). \\n - Once outside, you can move it freely on the canvas. \\n - If you still want grouping but not constraints, group (`⌘G` / `Ctrl+G`) instead of framing.\\n\\n4. **Flatten / detach** (if it’s a component or instance) \\n - If you’re working inside a component instance, you may not be able to freely move things. Right-click → **Detach Instance** first.\\n\\n👉 Quick check: if when you move the object, everything else shifts too, you’re inside an Auto Layout.
